 The central government has issued a gazette notification to regularize unauthorized colonies in Delhi
 is vinium kaa naam ' rashtriya rajdhani kshetra dilli ( anaadhikrut coloniyon main nivaasiyon ke sampatti ke adhikaron kii manyata) vinium 2019 naam diya gaya he
 Under this, 1731 colonies will be regularized in Delhi
 jabaki 69 prabhaavshaalee kaa rasukhdaar logon kii coloniyon ko niyamit nahin karne kii suchi main daalaa gaya he
 This was approved by the Central Government in the Cabinet last week and told that this step will benefit 40 lakh people of Delhi
 bataa den, kendriya awaasan or shahari kaary mantralay ne ye notification jari kiya he
 Durga Shankar Mishra, Secretary of this Ministry said in a tweet, 'I am happy that the gazette notification has been issued to provide ownership / transfer / mortgage rights to 40 lakh residents of 1731 unauthorized colonies of Delhi
 yah aage kii kaarywahi ke liye rasta banayega
 'this Gazette Notification is available on the weblink: https: / / t
 co / lpvibnauksjo colony 1 june 2014 ko astitv main thi, or 1 janvari 2015 ko 50% viksit thi yani usamen aabaadi thi unako hi pakkaa kiya jayega
 At present, there are 1731 such colonies which survive on this scale
 jabaki is paimaane par khari utarane vaali 69 coloniyaan aisi hai jinako dhani yaa rasukhdaar logon kii colony mana gaya he or isko niyamit nahin karne kaa faisla kiya gaya he
 Along with this, the DDA has been asked to consolidate the colonies (apart from the bloodbath) within 2 years
 saath hi didie ko yah bhi kaha gaya he ki aisi or coloniyon kii bhi pahchaan karen
 There are two types of categories based on the ground - 1
 Government or agricultural land that has been compensated
 2
 Private land
 sarkari zamin par bane makaan kaa malikana haq lene ke liye-1
 Plots below 100 meters - quarter of carpet area × 0 of circle rate
 5%2
 Plots of 100-250 meters - quarter of carpet area × 1% 3 of circle rate
 250 meter se upar plat - karpet aria kaa chauthai × cirkil rate kaa 2
 To take ownership of a house built on 5% private land, the applicant will have to pay half of the charge of the house built on the government land i
e
 50%
 1
 This charge will be valid for 1 year of notification, if delay is more than 1 year, there will be 8% late payment charge
 2
 Applicants will be able to pay the fees of the Registry in three installments
 3
 The applicant who will pay all the charges in one go will get immediate ownership
 4
 Provisional ownership will be given on payment of two-thirds, which will be converted into permanent ownership once the payment is completed
 5
 If someone tries to pay less by showing less of his property, he will have to pay the charge on all his property if caught
 yahaan tak ki us property ke liye bhi jis kaa malikana haq usko mil chukaa he
 6
 corpet aria ke aadhaar par charge liya jayega
 Circle rate i
e
 8 categories of residential areas A, B, C, D, E, F, G, H
 lekin ye niyamit coloniyon kii hoti he
 In such a situation, what would be the circle rate to register in unauthorized colony? For this, the category of the best-known colony of that area will be applied
 kisi bhi colony ko niyamit karne ke liye sabase zyada jaruri hoga uskaa nakshaa jo inaki boundry tay karegaa
 The DDA is tasked with drawing a boundary of these unauthorized colonies
 1
 DDA will create a web portal
 2
 The DDA will form a panel of agencies to determine the position of each house in the Jio Coordinates ie Google Map
 3
 Applicants first create their digilocker account and upload all their documents in it
 4
 Applicants should contact any of the agencies prescribed by the DDA to determine the Geo Coordinate of their house
 5
 The agency will decide the Geo Coordinate for the plot of the house
 agency vyakti ke plat kii or uske aasapaas kii auto- CAD drawing banaaegi
 The agency will then generate a QR code by uploading to Jio Coordinate and auto-cad Drawing Portal
 ye QR code aavedak ko diya jayega
 6
 aavedak didie ke portal par apane aap ko register karaayega7
 When the applicant will apply for the ownership, the basic information of the applicant and the property for which he has applied will be displayed on the website, so that if anyone has any objection, then they should register
 8
 After giving all the information online, after paying the payment, people of DDA will come for inspection
 iske liye khud aavedak hi taarikh or samay tay karegaa9
 DDA will complete the process of awarding the Conveyance deed or Authorization slip in 180 days, if there is any mistake or problem in the claim, DDA will cancel the application giving reasons 10

 The private plane carrying Shah Rukh Khan, Ambani and his group landed at White Plains Airport, 53 kilometers from Manhattan, at 1:30 pm
 sutron ne bataaya ki baaki sab ko to turant avrajan manjuuri de di gai, lekin shahrukh ko roak liya gaya or unhen dhai baje tak intjaar karnaa padaa
 The comments sutron ke anusaar white plance hawaii adda chota-sa he or jab tak shahrukh ko avrajan manjuuri nahin mil gai, samooh ke baaki sabhi log unka intjaar karte rahe
 Stopping Shah Rukh in this way, he and others of his party were greatly disturbed and were struggling to solve the problem
 samvaadadaata sammelan bees minute chalaa or is dauraan shahrukh ne unhen roke jane ke bare main kuch nahin kaha
 His team members and university officials also did not say anything about the reasons for his detention
 is bare main sampark kiye jane par shahrukh ne apane dal ke ek sadsy kii marfat kaha ki is prakaran par vah koi tippanee nahin karenge
 The member said that Shah Rukh's assertion that the US immigration officials expel his arrogance is a proof that he is deeply saddened by this incident
 sutron ne bataaya ki 46 varshiya abhinayta ko dopaher baad do baje ek samvaadadaata sammelan ko sambodhit karnaa tha or chaar baje vah yel vishvavidhyalay main vyaakhyaan dene vaale the haalanki vah samvaadadaata sammelan ke liye nirdhaarit samay se teen ghanta deree se pahunche or unka ek ghanta chalane vaala vyaakhyaan bhi shaam chah baje ke aasapaas shuru ho paaya
 Addressing the students at the university, Shah Rukh said, "whenever i feel proud of myself, i take a round of America
 yahaan ke avrajan adhikari meri sari hekdi nikaal dete hai
 Shahrukh said that even under such circumstances, he has a wealth of his small successes
 shahrukh ne kaha, ‘‘ vah (avrajan adhikari) hameshaa mujhase poochhate hai ki meraa kad kitna he or main hameshaa jhooth bolta hum ki meraa kad paanch foot das inch he
 Next time I'm going to be a little more adventurous
 (agar vah mujhase puuchhenge) meraa rang kya he to main kah duungaa gora
 '' sutron ne bataaya ki isse purv jab yah maaloom hua ki shahrukh ko neuyork ke white plance hawaii adde par roak liya gaya he to yel vishvavidhyalay ke adhikariyon ne washington sthit america avrajan or seemaa shulk vibhaag or aantarik suraksha vibhaag ke adhikariyon se is bare main sampark kiya
 He told that Shah Rukh Khan was very upset with this whole episode and it took the university authorities a long time to normalize him
 shahrukh bharat waapas laut aae hai
 He was awarded his prestigious Chubb Fellowship by the Connecticut Yale University
 faillowship ke antargat khan ne vishvavidhyalay ke saikadon chaatro, unke abhibhavako, faikalti or bharat america samudaay ke anya sadasyon ko yel parisar main sambodhit kiya

 ambani kii putree isha yel vishvavidhyalay main padhati he or vishvavidhyalay ke dakshin asian samaaj kii adhyaksh bhi he
 Khan said he was "detained" at the airport as usual
 ’’ shahrukh kaa sambodhan sunne aae logon ko jab yah maaloom hua ki unhen ek baar phir hawaii adde par roak liya gaya tha to vah log khaase hairaan hue or unhone america adhikariyon ko jeebhar kosa, lekin is sabase bekhbar bhartiya abhinayta ne kaha, ‘‘yah acha tha kyonki yah hameshaa hota he

 vishvavidhyalay main chaatro ko sambodhit karte hue shahrukh ne kaha, ‘‘ jab bhi mujhe khud par gumaan hone lagata he to main america kaa ek chakkar laga letaa hum

 ’’ shahrukh ne kaha ki is tarah ke halaat main bhi unke paas unki choti-choti safaltaaon kaa khajaana he

" agali baar main thodaa or dussahsee hone vaala hum
 (if he would ask me) What color am I, then i will say blond

 vah kehete hai ki unhone sochaa tha ki vah isamen mahaj kuch saptaah hi tik paaenge
 Encouraged by his win, Ashish said, "I never thought i would win this show
" maine sochaa ki main bas kuch saptaah tak isamen rah paaungaa or uske baad ise sambhaal nahin paaungaa
 But after that it kept happening week after week
 
 It is a wonderful feeling
 " Ashish is best known for his television serial 'rangarasiya'
 'jhalak
 
 ' kii final kadi shanivaar raat colors channel par prasaarit hui
 Ashish faced Mouni Roy, Shakti Mohan and Karan Tacker
 ashish ne kaha, "mauni or karan laajawab the
 He was my closest rival
 yahaan tak ki shakti jabardast thim
 i did not see a dancer like him
 " Ashish gives full credit for his victory to his fellow dance director Shampha Sonthalia
 ashish ne kaha, "main apni jeet kaa shrey apni nrity-nirdeshika shampa ko detaa hum
 " 'jhalak dikhalaa ja 7' ke vijeta ke rup main ashish ko 30 lakh rupee or mahindra eksyuvi car di gai

 is puure cond ke khulaase ke baad se hidilip vermafaraar tha magar aakhirkaar vah sibiai ke hathe chadh gaya
